data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">1</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;"><strong><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 18px;">儿童牙膏、牙刷、牙线怎么选？</span></strong></span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br></span></strong></p><section style="font-size: 16px;"><section style="margin: 10px 8px;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(255, 254, 254, 0);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);"><section style="line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;" powered-by="xiumi.us"><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q1 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：不同年龄的阶段如何选牙刷？牙刷头到底是大点好还是小点好？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这需要匹配孩子的牙弓和牙齿。有的孩子牙齿比较大，牙弓也挺宽大的，刷头可以适当大一点。有个评判标准可以参考：</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(64, 118, 0);">牙刷的刷头放在门牙上，差不多正好能盖住两颗门牙的大小为宜。</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">有的家长认为非要给孩子用儿童牙刷，儿童牙刷的刷毛不够长，这也大可不必。只要刷头能够盖住我们两颗牙的大小，刷毛长一点不要过软，最好刷毛的尖端是经过磨圆处理的，不伤害牙龈和牙釉质那就可以了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q2 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子可以用电动牙刷吗？几岁可以用？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">小朋友可以用电动牙刷，年龄没有限制。跟孩子沟通好了之后，哪怕是1岁多的孩子照样可以使用电动牙刷，它不是什么危险的工具。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">电动牙刷从原理上讲，分为两个流派：一个是旋转震动式的，一个是超声波式。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">旋转震动式的一般来说马达比较强，震动感比较强；</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 1.5em;"><iframe class="video_iframe rich_pages" data-vidtype="2" data-mpvid="wxv_2060159486207590401" data-cover="http%3A%2F%2Fmmbiz.qpic.cn%2Fmmbiz_jpg%2FswjqjmWVbWMV6YPIL33cZicusdAvLtd00nAB8oIVibhPE2jI6KVFklMG06BFMOEP6VhCYnBMKuo6iaXDEtiaIRdCGw%2F0%3Fwx_fmt%3Djpeg" allowfullscreen frameborder="0" data-ratio="2.0215384615384617" data-w="1314" data-src="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/mp/readtemplate?t=pages/video_player_tmpl&action=mpvideo&auto=0&vid=wxv_2060159486207590401"></iframe></p><p Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/ELbyuC3gEwDmc7GBJ6__3hM28oBstp_87hU_cTGcNytAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);">超声波式的震感没有那么强烈，孩子的接受度上，可能会好一些。</span></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><iframe class="video_iframe rich_pages" data-vidtype="2" 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">现在市面上也出了一些U型的电动牙刷，可以套在牙上，咬上之后整个全口都刷了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><br></span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;">U型电动牙刷我不是很推荐</span></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">，因为它和托盘差不多。其实每个孩子的牙弓的大小和形态都不太一样的，如果想要刷到位，我还是建议用常规的电动牙刷去清理。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q3 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：做过根管治疗、补过牙的乳牙，能用电动牙刷吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">可以。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q4 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：给小孩刷牙的时候转着圈儿刷就可以吗？还是必须上下斜着刷。如果用了电动牙刷还需要用“巴式刷牙法”吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果用电动牙刷能够把孩子的每颗牙都刷到，就不用再手动去刷了，因为让孩子去学改良巴式刷牙法有点儿难。我见过学“改良巴式刷牙法”最快的也是教了4、5次才学会的成年人。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我自己初学巴氏刷牙法的时候，刚开始也需要7、8分钟，所以找一个孩子合适的电动牙刷还是可以省不少力气的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section style="white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" data-galleryid data-ratio="0.8493150684931506" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">巴式刷牙法</span></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q5 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：10岁以下的小朋友由于手部的动作不够完善，所以牙的内侧、侧面会刷不好，如果孩子用电动牙刷，是不是就把它摆在那儿就可以了？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">摆在那儿就行了，一个位点差不多摆个四五秒就行了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">但牙菌斑不容易通过肉眼看到，我建议家长可以在网上购买一些</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(64, 118, 0);">碱性品红</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">的片剂，很便宜的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img" 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);">👆搜索“牙菌斑显示“就会出现很多产品<br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">你每周和孩子做一个游戏，孩子刷完牙之后，让他用碱性品红咀嚼一下，看看哪地方变红了，这样才能监督我们刷得好不好。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q6 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：涂上了碱性品红后能通过刷牙刷掉吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">只要把牙菌斑刷掉，牙齿就会变白。因为它染的是细菌，不会染染牙釉质。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q7 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：刷牙的时长是不是一定要刷够两分钟？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果用电动牙刷，我建议至少要用2分钟，可以外侧1分钟、里侧1分钟。电动牙刷一个周期的设置时常一般是2分钟。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">电牙刷无论是旋转、机械震颤，都比我们人手的震颤频率要高一些。如果家长怕孩子刷得不够，可以采用两个周期。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q8 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子几岁可以自己刷牙？有没有什么技巧让孩子能够好好刷牙？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我建议3岁以内的孩子，需要家长帮忙刷牙。3岁以后，孩子能够明白事情了，家长陪着孩子刷。</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(64, 118, 0);">10岁再让孩子完全独立刷牙</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。孩子的口腔护理需要家长重视起来。家长需要自己养成一个很好的口腔习惯，给孩子以身作则。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q9 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：儿童牙膏怎么挑？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;">牙膏之间的主要差距在摩擦剂，</span></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">稍微贵点的牙膏和便宜牙膏最重要的就是摩擦剂的差异，还有就是发泡剂。很多牙膏的发泡剂非常大，稍微一沾水满嘴的泡沫，这会给孩子一种感觉：有这么多泡沫，我的牙是不是已经四处都刷到了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">所以</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(64, 118, 0);">我建议最好用泡沫小一点的，摩擦剂质量好一点的牙膏。</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">特别便宜的牙膏也不是不能用，但</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;">如果讲究一点还是硅剂的摩擦剂</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">，就好比有些便宜的牙膏里面的摩擦剂颗粒大小不均匀，很多细小的颗粒在显微镜下都是非常尖锐的，它其实损伤牙齿表面的光洁度。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">好的摩擦剂中的颗粒大小相对比较均匀，并且表面是经过处理的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q10 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友觉得牙膏辣，说能不能不用牙膏刷牙，这可以吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">拿干牙刷刷，只要刷得足够认真，也是可以的。牙膏主要是通过提高摩擦力进而提高我们清除牙菌斑的效率的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q11 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子老是吃牙膏怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">建议家长在孩子不能自主吞咽之前不要给他用含氟牙膏，很多氟对身体是不好的，孩子刷牙的时候大部分就直接把牙膏吃了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这在牙膏盒的配料上都会有标注。如果家长对孩子更上心的话，可以每三个月、半年给他涂氟保护漆，氟保护漆在牙齿表面保持的时间更久，比氟泡沫的持久性更好。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q12 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：多大的孩子能用牙线？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">只要孩子有了两颗相邻的牙齿就可以用牙线。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q13 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：牙线怎么挑？小朋友的牙线就是小号的大人牙线吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">基本上只要是选购正规厂商的就可以。不管牙线打没打蜡、加没加薄荷，这些都不重要，重要的是我们用牙线的手法。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">小孩的牙线没有什么特别的。孩子的牙缝比大人的牙缝还要大，所以牙线没有什么特别可纠结的。如果孩子觉得牙线不太好用的话，可以买有手柄的牙线棒。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section #电动牙刷 #牙齿矫正" data-nonceid="16010907150517656836" data-type="video"></mpvideosnap></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q14 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：牙线用了以后流血怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这种情况可能是几个原因导致的：</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">第一是他的牙龈是有炎症。健康的牙龈是质地粉红，坚韧，除非用暴力，否则它真的不那么容易出血。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">第二才有可能是我们的牙线使用方法不当，这种情况下，我建议去洗牙。洗完牙再请牙医指导一下。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">所以如果用牙线有出血的情况，我的建议是先去洗牙，再说牙线的使用方式。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q15 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：用牙线会扩大牙缝吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">正常使用牙线是不会扩大牙缝的，大部分情况下我们的牙缝里其实就是之前残存的菜叶、食物残渣、牙菌斑、牙结石。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q16 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友用牙线的时候有的牙缝放不进去怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">可以学习一下牙线的使用方法，乳牙牙缝比较大，除非严重拥挤都能放进去。所以乳牙放不进去，基本上都是我们手法的问题。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q17 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：牙线和牙缝刷一样吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙缝刷是牙缝足够大的时候用的，牙线是牙缝不够大的时候用的，它们的作用是一样的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙周炎、牙龈萎缩得比较严重的情况要用牙缝刷，牙线的效率清洁就就稍微弱了一些。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q18 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：能买洗牙器自己给小孩洗牙吗？洗牙器能不能取代牙刷、牙线？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">洗牙虽然不算技术含量特别高的一项操作，但它还是有一点门槛的。洗牙器有水，有它的震动频率、和牙齿的接触面积、接触时间的要求，这些需要非常严格的专业培训才可以正确操作。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们自己可能买了一些并不正规洗牙的工具自己操作，或许能够清除一部分牙结石，但还是挺伤害牙釉质的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q19 </span></strong><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;">：小朋友需要用漱口水吗？</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子可以不用漱口水。如果非要用的话，可以用那些主要成分是精油的这种漱口水，千万不要用广谱的抑菌杀菌成分的漱口水。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q20 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：冲牙器能不能每天用？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我建议每天使用刷牙、牙线、冲牙器三套一起使用，它们的功能还是不一样的。</span></p></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">2</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;">窝沟封闭、涂氟、洗牙等日常护理</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q21 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：有必要给孩子做窝沟封闭吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">窝沟封闭降低了牙齿窝沟发生龋面的风险。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">窝沟封闭基本上都用于孩子的后牙，比如乳磨牙，还有恒磨牙和恒牙中的前磨牙。因为我们后牙的牙尖，从牙胚的时候就是几个部分融合在一起的。但能够融合得特别完美人的是极少数，大部分都会在显微镜下有一些可见的微小裂隙。我们通过使用比补牙材料流动性更好一点的树脂基质材料，把缝隙给封闭上，减少细菌通过窝沟进去产生龋坏的可能性。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">由于窝沟封闭的推广，现在孩子最常见的龋坏其实不是窝沟了，而是临牙之间牙间隙的部分。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q22 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子3岁，想问下多大的孩子可以做窝沟封闭？是不是在乳牙期只做一次就可以？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">差不多乳牙期做一次就可以。3岁孩子的乳磨牙就可以做窝沟封闭了。窝沟封闭基本都是免费的，全国的牙防所、指定机构都可以免费做的，家长如果不怕排队的话，基本上就没必要再花额外的钱。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q23 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子6岁了，长了两颗恒牙，是不是要做窝沟封闭？窝沟封闭是按颗算的，所以长出了是不是就可以做了？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">只要我们的恒牙完全萌出了，可以长一颗做一颗恒牙的窝沟封闭，越早越好。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q24 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：哪里能查询免费做窝沟封闭的定点医院的信息？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">家长可以搜索任何一个地区的牙防所。比如北京、上海地区都有口腔医院，口腔医院的预防科就可以免费做。包括北京、上海的各个区医院的口腔科其实也有。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">其实政府对于窝沟封闭、涂氟的免费服务已经实施了好多年。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q25 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：口气问题怎么改良？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">产生口气有两种情况：第一是口腔的问题，第二是消化道的问题。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">需要我们好好刷牙、用牙线，每天坚持刷舌头。舌头是凸起结构，上面有好多绒毛，它的上皮代谢非常快，会有很多细菌。所以用专门的硅胶制品或者很软的软毛牙刷刷舌头，口气能够改善很多。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">当然还有一种口气是全身系统的疾病引起的，很多其他系统的疾病都会有一些病理性的口气，像糖尿病。如果上面清洁口腔的步骤都做了，还有口气，就要对对症地处理包括一些消化道的问题。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 16px;"> Q26 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);">：小朋友几岁能开始洗牙，怎么给小朋友洗牙？和大人的流程一样吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">按照美国儿童口腔医学会的建议，孩子长牙之后基本都可以洗牙。但因为孩子的唾液分泌非常旺盛，乳牙期可以不洗牙。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">从孩子长第一颗牙开始，我们就应该进行口腔护理。并且家长最好能够陪伴、监督孩子刷牙，一直到孩子10岁，这是德国人的建议。在德国人看来，10岁的孩子才普遍有较好的自控力。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">为什么孩子自己有可能刷不好牙呢？</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section style="white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.7426160337552743" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/KNinS_Z64feNdQO6GL9nzJqaa3xBQrxYbZSqWsXr4LjaAQAAYAEAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="height: 249px;width: 335px;" normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/IR33r7UIUmXIGuycrRhpL3vwA3GSTcYnu6Kry5SP1KhAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/IR33r7UIUmXIGuycrRhpL3vwA3GSTcYnu6Kry5SP1KhAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">牙菌斑</span></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这是一张很常见的孩子的牙齿状态。仔细看的话，我们就会发现是在牙齿的龈缘水平有一些看起来似乎不太干净的物质，但这么来看还可以。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section style="white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.7544303797468355" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/Ox_9E3B3s-dsmmKi-9a0XTzBOpqzvK1TSO0DgsjHEmiLAQAAKgEAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="395" style="height: 263px;width: 348px;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/Ox_9E3B3s-dsmmKi-9a0XTzBOpqzvK1TSO0DgsjHEmiLAQAAKgEAAEpQ.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/qM7kIdANlTMluD-sPb5Z9jqtFnOZq6o8InYcwY_8DUlAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/qM7kIdANlTMluD-sPb5Z9jqtFnOZq6o8InYcwY_8DUlAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">菌斑测试技下的牙菌斑</span></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这是涂了菌斑指示剂后的图片。菌斑指示剂可以让牙菌斑显示出来的，人们刷过牙之后用过菌斑指示剂后显示出的红色部分就是牙菌斑。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><section style="white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="1.3605442176870748" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/sbChEW4h3_LyJQW5-P3zO4hPs0jQQBo-xVzhK2Gtm6NMAgAAIAMAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="588" style="height: 351px;width: 258px;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/sbChEW4h3_LyJQW5-P3zO4hPs0jQQBo-xVzhK2Gtm6NMAgAAIAMAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/755" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/5Jnvs_FmLNteaocQutnQPuebaWYBf0jW_Zs-Y5ol3JNAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/5Jnvs_FmLNteaocQutnQPuebaWYBf0jW_Zs-Y5ol3JNAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">牙菌斑的电镜照片</span></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙菌斑在我们牙齿上附着，好比我们的墙面上长的一些藤蔓植物、苔藓似的，简单的刷牙是很难刷干净的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q27 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子牙齿涂氟可以自主进行吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);">涂氟要严格按照医生的建议去做</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。特别不建议有些家长过于热心，比如我们建议氟保护期3个月、半年再用一次，家长恨不得每礼拜用一次。孩子还小，他会吞咽的，吞咽之后就会全身用氟。有一个病叫氟骨症，所以涂氟这件事我们严格的按照医生的建议就好了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q28 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：已经吃了很多牙含氟牙膏咋办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">那就别再吃了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">3</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="font-size: 18px;letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子有龋齿怎么办？</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section style="font-size: 16px;"><section style="margin: 10px 8px;line-height: 2em;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(255, 254, 254, 0);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);"><section powered-by="xiumi.us"><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q29 </strong></span><strong> </strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子先天脱矿严重，很容易产生龋齿，现在每3个月定期涂氟坚持刷牙，但是挨着牙龈的部分怎么都刷不干净，怎么办？</span></strong></section><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">第一，已经脱矿的部分不会因为刷牙就复原；第二，刷得干不干净用碱性品红去测试就可以。脱矿的部分再怎么刷牙菌斑，都很难完全复原，只要它不再进展就好了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q30 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：自己在家给孩子涂氟可以吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">在家涂氟也是没有问题的，在严格的产品寿命内都是可以的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">但是涂氟不是我们孩子不患龋齿的充分条件，它只是一个额外附加条件。如果想孩子不患龋齿，最好还是严格的刷好牙，用好牙线，清洁好牙缝，因为乳牙的牙缝比恒牙的牙缝相对而言还是要大一点。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子的龋齿最常见的是从牙缝的地方开始坏。因为成人塞牙之后，晚上会弄出来。孩子忘性大，适应能力也强，塞了牙之后就忘了，这块儿肉在龋齿的牙缝中待的时间久了，就坏牙了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">为了避免这种情况的发生，家长最好每天监督孩子刷牙。孩子长牙之后，每天家长亲自用牙线把孩子的牙缝过一遍。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q31 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：三岁宝宝的牙</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">齿上有白色的斑点，这是为什么呢？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">基本上白色的斑点那个就是早期龋坏，我们俗称的这个白垩斑，出现了白垩斑之后一定要强化好好刷牙，局部涂氟。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我见过有些家长为了哄孩子省心，每天晚上让孩子抱着奶瓶喝奶入睡，觉得这样好省心，可时间久了孩子全口20颗乳牙做了20个根管治疗，这就是奶瓶龋。所以不要让孩子的牙每天晚上在糖水里泡着，包括吃夜奶。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.8384615384615385" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/-7OOlDsTKhpCrIvTkZ0_zL8_gdy1kN7VrVfkSu-8VOaGAQAARwEAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="390" style="font-size: 16px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/-7OOlDsTKhpCrIvTkZ0_zL8_gdy1kN7VrVfkSu-8VOaGAQAARwEAAEpQ.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.5709515859766278" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/ALBhQ_oENXYdqWBbzqVKeVPYbBoe_IFU6C80kZbKgzA4BAAAaQIAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="1198" style="height: 222px;font-size: 16px;text-align:
