referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/-PJRmzt-kHSjhT07vCeq-JQd9SoAvpfvajM79tic16RAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/-PJRmzt-kHSjhT07vCeq-JQd9SoAvpfvajM79tic16RAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);">白垩斑</span></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> Q32 </span></strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：16个月的小孩儿牙齿外内侧都有点儿黑，外侧的就能刷掉，内侧还有黑的，医生说是虫牙不要紧，请问是这样吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果是确定是虫牙就不可能不要紧。如果牙齿已经黑了能补赶紧补。孩子有了龋齿不能说不管它。</span></p><p style="text-align: center;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q33 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：儿保的时候医生让做龋齿基因检测，有必要吗？为什么有些小朋友吃很多糖仍然不会得龋齿？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">其实没有必要。龋病是细菌引起的慢性的感染性疾病，要做的就是做好口腔清洁，不给细菌生长的温床。即便检测出不易感龋齿，如果不好好刷牙、做好口腔护理，依旧会患龋。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">的确有个别小朋友口腔里面的致龋菌比较少，但还是要做好口腔护理。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q34 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子的乳牙因为龋齿脱落了，需要等恒牙长出再治疗吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这取决于孩子的年龄，如果孩子现在2-4岁，3、4年后才会长出恒牙。这种情况我建议治疗。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">首先，孩子没有门牙在幼儿园可能会被小朋友取笑或起外号；</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">第二，如果孩子年纪过小龋齿很严重，如果不治疗炎症，炎症会顺着牙根儿往牙槽骨里发展。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">第三，牙根在骨头里是为了稳固并且引导牙槽骨发育的，如果过早地拔除，这个作用也会起不到。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果孩子已经6岁了，乳牙牙根已经吸收一半或1/3，这个时候坏了可以等待恒牙长出。但如果孩子很小的时候，建议还要医治。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q35 </strong></span><strong> </strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子的门牙面上突然掉了一个小洞，是缺钙引起的吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;"><strong><br></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这一定是龋齿，全身补钙治不了龋齿。再次强调，龋齿是细菌引起的慢性疾病，预防措施就是好好刷牙，治疗龋齿就要看牙医，补钙没有效果。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;"> Q36 </span></strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小孩儿的牙缝蛀了怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">补牙就可以。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q37 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友有龋齿不配合牙医治疗怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">还是要去看牙医。家长可以通过一些方法减轻孩子的恐惧感，比如给孩子看动画片分散注意力、尽量把治疗过程需要经历什么给孩子提前讲清楚等。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">日常生活里，有一些家长会拿医生、警察去吓唬孩子，这特别不好。</span><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;">应该告诉孩子牙医、警察，或者任何一个其专业人士都是在帮助他，是跟他是一伙的。采用正确的方式引导，3岁以上的孩子，10个里面8个都是可以沟通的。 </span></p></section></section></section></section><section style="line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;"><br></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">4</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t">孩子没有龋齿，为什么牙那么黑？</p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q38 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友的牙齿很容易变黑怎么办？1岁半的小朋友牙齿上有很多小黑点，牙齿和牙龈交界处特别多，这些是不是都是牙菌斑？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">小朋友牙齿变黑基本上有两种可能：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">一个是真的是龋坏，也就是我们常说的“坏牙”。</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">但这种情况基本上除了变黑，还有色、形、质的改变：它的形态会发生改变，它的质地比较软。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">还有一种常见的情况就是纯粹的色素。</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">有些家长说，孩子这么小不抽烟、不喝茶，怎么会有这么多色素呢？其实这是个误区。像我每天三四杯咖啡，但我的牙齿并没有色素，可能就是我口腔里面的产黑色素杆菌含量比较少。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们可以给家长看下什么是龋坏：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><section style="text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.624" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/IxOasAjOiqM9gf5Sn4iO1dz_AkJJuYaQfK4CqV7t21T0AQAAOAEAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="500" style="width: 393px;height: 245px;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/IxOasAjOiqM9gf5Sn4iO1dz_AkJJuYaQfK4CqV7t21T0AQAAOAEAAEpQ.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/h5iW_AiPkbptxixxMaN58lr8w2UxGVCTfIazp26VOZtAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/h5iW_AiPkbptxixxMaN58lr8w2UxGVCTfIazp26VOZtAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">儿童龋齿</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">龋坏不仅变黑了，还有形态的改变。并且它是软的，我们用仪器都能扎得进去。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们再看一下什么是色素：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section style="text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="1.1003937007874016" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/GvASPIL_7j6LooOzGJzki84flAF1Xo6h6PEDv0VKH9z8AQAALwIAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="508" style="width: 284px;height: 313px;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/GvASPIL_7j6LooOzGJzki84flAF1Xo6h6PEDv0VKH9z8AQAALwIAAEpQ.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/zTjdQLThkZXJhDUTNdRtVlrjCFEN8O-EcNbqSZtV5NNAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/zTjdQLThkZXJhDUTNdRtVlrjCFEN8O-EcNbqSZtV5NNAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">色素沉着</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">小牙还是白的，但上面的污浊就像烟斑茶渍似的，这个是色素。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">龋坏基本上是因为细菌、糖分以及我们的牙菌斑在这段时间里造成了牙齿的腐坏。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section style="white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-ratio="0.668" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/FIC2q9KpOWLc1GZLHDpYinBV21NyyLDbVkyx6oMEqSv6AAAApwAAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="250" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/FIC2q9KpOWLc1GZLHDpYinBV21NyyLDbVkyx6oMEqSv6AAAApwAAAEpQ.jpg" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/zqYBTFKVoxers9gfiBQmSoRnZWqaUH5ZycVaUckt27NAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/zqYBTFKVoxers9gfiBQmSoRnZWqaUH5ZycVaUckt27NAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">产黑色素杆菌</span></section><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><br></span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">色素沉着则真的因人而异，有的小朋友的口腔菌群结构里面的产黑色素杆菌比较多，它自己能够产出色素，一般这种情况下小朋友洗牙抛光就好了，龋坏的话可能需要补。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section class="channels_iframe_wrp"><mpvideosnap class="js_uneditable custom_select_card channels_iframe" data-pluginname="videosnap" data-id="export/UzFfAgtgekIEAQAAAAAAP9oL_RpWbwAAAAstQy6ubaLX4KHWvLEZgBPE84IcO1Q0S-P9zNPgMItLzi_6sz7mEyqHoE21EDv8" data-url="https://findermp.video.qq.com/251/20304/stodownload?encfilekey=rjD5jyTuFrIpZ2ibE8T7YmwgiahniaXswqzLfNQS8J28BekeX0RZo6JnqC14lntE4PbD3WfzHyiaRozcic8mXr1scV5mARVERgU2urhicVWvHRhP8&adaptivelytrans=0&bizid=1023&dotrans=0&hy=SH&idx=1&m=&token=AxricY7RBHdX9EDvKdxjGLJJmuQSDpWlpic66lfF7ibIprItgeRTXMAQJOiaytkdkUOqpKgqDq0qavc" #牙齿矫正" data-nonceid="13920534891469014130" data-type="video"></mpvideosnap></section><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;text-align: justify;"> </span><br><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"></span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q39 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：色素沉淀通过洗牙可以清除吗？经常抛光对孩子的牙齿有没有影响？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">色素和牙结石刷不掉，只能让牙医用专业设备清除。色素可以通过洗牙抛光去除。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子牙齿的抛光顶多半年、一年进行一次，抛光的药水属于微米级的，基本可以认为对牙齿的影响忽略不计。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q40 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：7岁小朋友可以洗牙吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">肯定是可以的。我们遇到一个2、3岁的小朋友在幼儿园感到很自卑，因为口腔色素比较多，他的确实口腔产生的黑素杆菌太茂盛了，不到半年满嘴就跟抽烟喝茶似的，他妈说我们家孩子这么小怎么这么油腻呢？</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">其实就是色素比较多。洗牙没有一定的严格要求，如果色素比较多了，影响美观了，清除就好了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q41 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子5岁还没有换牙，牙齿有黑色，但是没有蛀牙，洗过一次很快又发现了一点黑色，要怎么预防和清理？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子口腔里产黑色素的杆菌比较旺盛，是没什么办法的。只有等孩子的牙齿黑了我们再抛光，再清洗。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">其实每个孩子生下来的时候，它的口腔里面都是无菌的，孩子口腔的细菌和妈妈的产道的菌群结构是有关系的，跟家庭成员的菌群结构也是有关系的。所以这个孩子的菌群结构，是和他出生的家庭的进食有关的。这也是为什么我们建议给孩子的分餐制的原因。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q42 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：为什么孩子每天刷牙牙还是会变黄，牙齿颜色的正常的范畴是什么呢？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">从乳牙到开始换恒牙的时候，家长都会很担心：孩子现在牙又大又黄又丑，怎么办？但乳牙本来就比恒牙白一些。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">原因是乳牙的牙釉质矿化不完全，牙釉质的透亮度没有那么高。恒牙的矿化程度比较高，牙釉质是半透明的。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙釉质里面的牙本质是淡黄色的，恒牙透露的淡黄色就是牙本质的颜色，所以成年人的牙是偏淡黄色的。孩子的换牙期恒牙和乳牙的对比之下会显得牙齿发黄。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">而这个阶段孩子的颌骨还在发育，恒牙比换牙期的颌骨要大一些，所以显得牙齿比较大，没那么美观。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q43 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子1岁半，有色素牙能带去洗牙吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">可以洗牙。不过1岁半的小朋友的色素不用洗，抛光就好了。抛光可以不用水，孩子感受到的刺激会小一点。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">5</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 18px;">牙齿乳牙、恒牙缺失怎么办？</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section style="font-size: 16px;"><section style="margin: 10px 8px;line-height: 2em;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(255, 254, 254, 0);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);"><section powered-by="xiumi.us"><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q44 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：三岁孩子缺牙两颗，两岁去医院检查医生说无法拍片，请问几岁治疗合适？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">如果孩子的牙是先天缺失</span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">，那没有办法，只能说孩子长恒牙的时候看一下是不是也缺失，以及会不会孩子的恒牙没有缺失，但因为乳牙的缺失导致牙齿萌出的异常。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这时需要提前进行精细化管理，一般先天性缺失的是前牙，而</span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">前牙的先天性缺失影响不大</span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。如果缺失的是乳后牙，大概率会引起牙齿的拥挤或者不正常。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q45 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友的乳牙中两个虎牙都没有，今年要换牙了就拍了牙片，发现恒牙的牙胚在，这种情况需要注意吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">乳牙的缺失导致恒牙的过早萌出，因为上面没有乳牙的遮挡，就需要找牙医做好替牙期的间隙管理。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q46 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：5岁的孩子拍了牙片儿发现恒牙缺了两颗上牙该怎么处理？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">先天缺失没有什么特别好的办法，只能说</span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">等孩子换完牙后做好间隙管理</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。等萌出之后：</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style="width: 577.422px;white-space: normal;"><li><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果说孩子剩下的牙基本上都把缝都能占上，都不用干预；</span></p></li><li><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果缝没占完，但缝不大，我们可以通过矫正把小缝关上；</span></p></li><li><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果缝足够大，将来矫正完成后有可能会需要种牙。</span></p></li></ul><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q47 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子4岁磕了门牙，这时候需要补吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">4岁的孩子门牙大概率是乳磨牙。一般的牙外伤中如果牙的位置没有变，只是牙冠的破损。但从远期的角度来看，我们需要警惕乳牙会不会发生牙髓坏死。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">有时候孩子磕一下，当时什么事儿没有，但是牙齿和牙槽骨都是有弹性的，有可能乳牙在受伤的一瞬间发生了比较大的位移，随后它又复位了。这时候有可能孩子的牙齿神经血管处扯断了，时间久了就会牙髓坏死。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">牙髓坏死一般是无痛无知觉的</span></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">，再进一步有可能会引起根尖的感染，感染比较严重的话牙齿上会鼓个脓包。我们最好不要等到那一步，有可能会影响到孩子恒牙的萌出。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">所以只要有牙外伤，不管是乳牙的牙外伤还是恒牙的牙外伤都需要定期监测外伤牙的牙髓活力，避免它发生了坏死后，由于我们没有知觉一直让炎症在骨头里面去蔓延。它会腐蚀侵蚀牙槽骨，甚至会破坏恒牙的牙胚。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q48 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：6岁的孩子有一颗上门牙掉了，2个多月后新的还没萌出，这个要干预吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">6岁两颗上门牙掉了，上门牙差不多也是该萌出的状态了。我觉得需要再观察，如果3、4个月或者半年内孩子的口腔内还没有看到上牙冠，可以再拍一个片子评估下。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q49 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：6岁的孩子少了下牙的两侧第3颗牙齿正常吗？医生说没关系，就是少颗牙。</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这是乳尖牙，乳尖牙是先天缺失还是过早脱落，从这个描述中我没有听清。一般先天缺失乳侧切牙或者乳切牙比较常见，先天缺乳尖牙非常罕见，我觉得可以拍片子看一眼，明确看它是先天缺失还是完全埋伏。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q50 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子9个月了，长了两颗牙，上面没长牙，而且上面的牙龈都不明显，好像没牙龈似的。是没长好吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br></span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">9个月萌出两个下中切牙，这很正常，家长不要过于着急。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q51</span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：7周岁的孩子至今只换过两颗下门牙，需要干预吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><br></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">虽然有一个孩子换牙的时间表，但它只是一个参考。但实际生活中，差个半年一年，前后顺序有出入，要不是孩子先天缺牙，这都很正常。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><section style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/lAN-OroIP_5ahUTBWPbkqKxzHfiELO7Hx2HS-0rfSApAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64"
