referrerpolicy="no-referrer">恒牙萌出时间</span></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, "PingFang SC";font-weight: bold;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">6</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 18px;">什么情况下，孩子需要尽早去正畸？</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style> Q52 </span></strong><span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;">：孩子有点地包天，最早什么时候去正畸？什么情况需要尽早正畸？</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">只要出现了以下的几种情况，我都建议家长们还是带孩子去看一看：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">1、个别牙的反颌</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">不管是乳牙、恒牙，一定要及早找牙医。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子的面中部和面下部的发育，尤其是面中部，是前颌骨在牙齿的引导下完成的。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果发育中孩子的下牙限制住了上牙，这就是我们说的反颌。在孩子生长发育期的时候，会因为牙齿影响到前颌骨的发育。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">哪怕是单颗牙的反颌，只要发现了及早去看牙医，否则孩子的容貌会因为反颌发生变化。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="334" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.57734375" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/g44OXGcgxYtsXY6jCcWM5TQXUIEYD0Vh3kxkN91z8XE4BAAAcAIAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="1280" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/g44OXGcgxYtsXY6jCcWM5TQXUIEYD0Vh3kxkN91z8XE4BAAAcAIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/320" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/Q7TXAp5h10gNV43ztGTxvdzPafmScIkdHbYJBp9i8_1AAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/Q7TXAp5h10gNV43ztGTxvdzPafmScIkdHbYJBp9i8_1AAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);">个别牙反颌</span><br></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">2、比较明显的外突和深覆盖</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">刚刚也提到上颌骨的发育主要是前颌骨的发育，前颌骨的发育是在牙齿的引导下完成的，所以要对牙齿进行及早的干预。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">包括这种其实是稍微骨性的：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="317" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.54921875" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/d9g23JVaOtbeLA75Ld3u_qxm_efqRkmfHvH5v2d2lLk4BAAAUQIAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="1280" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/d9g23JVaOtbeLA75Ld3u_qxm_efqRkmfHvH5v2d2lLk4BAAAUQIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/304" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/-C1rRNzk0BiCSDV8WhIc4luYHqQBc7drT8RpizVuhcBAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/-C1rRNzk0BiCSDV8WhIc4luYHqQBc7drT8RpizVuhcBAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;">上牙前凸</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">龅牙在比较早的时期进行干预，孩子换完牙或者成年以后的情况就会改善很多：乳齿有这种情况，恒牙即便是有也会变成简单的问题，否则问题积攒到最后可能变得很复杂。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">3、开颌问题</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子先天舌体肥大，或者喜欢嘬手指头，导致牙咬合不上，就会产生开颌的问题。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="384" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.664" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/c00EnEaxwTP3wzDvJ9VJW4VuBr__cK3yr09y1pIhZc3oAwAAmAIAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1000" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/c00EnEaxwTP3wzDvJ9VJW4VuBr__cK3yr09y1pIhZc3oAwAAmAIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/368" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/7HVt320Q8V27Vi6K51BIO4xV7VcuT0VAe8QHFmS8NClAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/7HVt320Q8V27Vi6K51BIO4xV7VcuT0VAe8QHFmS8NClAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">牙齿开颌</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这也需要我们及早干预，否则牙齿会产生扭转。扭转牙齿的位置不对，别的牙位置也会不对。只有把扭转的牙齿转过来，位置摆对，其他的牙才会陆续有位置。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">4、严重的深覆合</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙齿看着整齐，但他的整个下牙都被盖得死死的，这种也是需要干预。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="378" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.654" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/40gQCMZiFm9306mbfaHGt5VrXlP1wuR8YXM84kfjmV_oAwAAjgIAAEpQ.jpg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1000" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/40gQCMZiFm9306mbfaHGt5VrXlP1wuR8YXM84kfjmV_oAwAAjgIAAEpQ.jpg?imageView2/1/w/555/h/362" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/fxXjBF788Ot2SzjrMSDw2bA5LzxLU79Wgs-oDIP9tlhAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/fxXjBF788Ot2SzjrMSDw2bA5LzxLU79Wgs-oDIP9tlhAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer">深覆合</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">5、后牙的反颌或后牙锁合</span></strong></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们刚刚展示的前牙，更隐蔽的是后牙的反颌或后牙锁合，家长根本自己发现不了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 1.5em;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="326" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.5638506876227898" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/wgSG2XkxkB_R0HlkmD2dJsjzL5XxLcky8RjthQaoBe76AwAAPgIAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="1018" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/wgSG2XkxkB_R0HlkmD2dJsjzL5XxLcky8RjthQaoBe76AwAAPgIAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/312" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></p><section style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5em;"><img data-ratio="1" data-src="https://2-im.guokr.com/zz72U9mxJi5oomczm_2N4Teylk24magX-qKx28rv12NAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="64" style="height: 20px !important;max-height: 20px !important;width: 20px !important;" src="https://2-im.guokr.com/zz72U9mxJi5oomczm_2N4Teylk24magX-qKx28rv12NAAAAAQAAAAFBO.png" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);">反颌</span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果是乳牙是锁合或者反颌的，恒牙长出来之后大概率也是锁合或者反颌的，将来孩子单侧的咀嚼功能基本上丧失了一大半，导致偏侧咀嚼，孩子将来的脸会长歪。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q53 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：乳牙期的孩子要不要做正畸？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">乳牙期也需要去看牙医，乳牙期孩子的颌骨也在发育。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">还是要强调，孩子前牙的反颌，后牙的反颌，后牙的锁合、扭转，严重的深覆盖这些其实都应该早期干预。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q54 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：正常牙齿咬合的图片是怎样的呢？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这是正常的咬合情况，它的覆盖关系、凸度，都是比较正常的。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section style="line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><img data-backh="345" data-backw="562" data-ratio="0.6138279932546374" data-src="https://3-im.guokr.com/SK1o4kBoTxmaON0ZQwpUB7p-QEiKNYHsNhYDLNw2SR1RAgAAbAEAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="593" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://3-im.guokr.com/SK1o4kBoTxmaON0ZQwpUB7p-QEiKNYHsNhYDLNw2SR1RAgAAbAEAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/340" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></span></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">很遗憾的是，对于大多数人来说，牙齿咬合不好的情况是会大概率发生的。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q55 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小朋友如果去正畸，也会像成年人这么痛苦吗？他能接受得了吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果孩子配合的话，用活动矫治器基本上就都可以解决，这个力量还是比较轻的。就我们过往介入的案例而言，孩子适应能力其实比成人还强。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q56 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子换牙期怎么戴牙套，牙齿突然掉了怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子乳牙列替牙期的干预和恒牙不一样，专业的医生给孩子设计矫正的时候都会考虑到他将来恒牙的萌出顺序，间隙、空间的保持，孩子的换牙、掉牙都会在制定方案的时候都考虑进去。孩子遵循医嘱戴牙套就可以了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q57 </strong></span><strong> </strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子7岁，在替牙期新长出的恒牙是里出外进的，是不是以后逃不出正畸的命运？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><br></span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果说想让孩子以后的矫正变得简单，或者孩子的面部发育受影响小，这时候其实就应该去评估，去看早期做点什么事情能够降低将来孩子换完牙之后正畸的难度。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q58 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：恒牙长出来有点歪怎么办？是要等牙齿全部换完再去矫正吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这个要看牙齿歪的程度，还是要找牙医当面评估。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q59 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子6岁半，上牙换了之后上牙突出，有点包牙，很多医院都说男孩11岁再整牙，应该去找什么样的医院来提出什么样的建议和方案？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">刚刚我展示过几种情况，不要说11岁了，3岁就要开始干预了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">并不是所有的牙医给出的所有建议都是正确的，并不是所有的牙医的理念都是一样的，我也没有办法具体推荐。哪怕在同一家三甲医院，牙医的知识更新速度不一样，可能给出的建议也不一样。家长们也确实挺不容易的，我们自己定期更新一些知识就好了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q60 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：正畸有好几种方案，那对于孩子推荐哪种呢？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">无论托槽还是隐形，最重要的是孩子配合。托槽最担心的是把孩子的牙毁了，隐形的最担心是孩子不好好带，把治疗周期拉得很漫长。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">如果佩戴隐形牙套，家长怕孩子自己抠掉，不够自律。隐形牙套最不适的，是前两三副。佩戴者酸胀甚至酸痛的不适非常明显。有些孩子可能过不了这个适应期，偷偷的把牙套抠掉。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">钢牙虽然是粘上去的，孩子自己抠不下来，但还有另外一个常见的问题：青春期能好好刷牙的孩子寥寥无几，孩子那个时候比较叛逆，要和大人的话反着干。如果这样，基本上会在托槽的周围会形成一层密密麻麻的牙菌斑，拆托槽的时候孩子的牙基本就废掉了。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">所以</span><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">在给孩子做正畸之前，家长、牙医还有孩子三方需要充分的沟通</span></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。孩子能够充分理解、充分配合，再开始。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q61 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：恒牙长出来就有牙缝需要干预吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">在换牙的过程中恒牙有牙缝是正常的。就怕在替牙期，牙没换完的时候，每颗牙长出来都严丝合缝的，挤得非常严实。这样大概率将来它是没有空间把牙都都排齐的。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q62 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子牙还没换齐，但是牙缝有半颗牙那么大，这个是要紧吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子如果是两个门牙的牙缝，并且还比较早期，倒也正常。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q63 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：腺样体肥大会影响牙齿生长吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">腺样体肥大会导致孩子口呼吸。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子张嘴睡觉会导致舌肌和口唇肌没有建平衡，导致孩子上牙弓的狭窄，下颌的发育不足，可能会导致孩子牙齿不齐。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="410" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.7095709570957096" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/JnbnBhJe41BUqudc01YMQYE3fDHECb_RgKtWngviFUteAgAArgEAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="606" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/JnbnBhJe41BUqudc01YMQYE3fDHECb_RgKtWngviFUteAgAArgEAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/393" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><strong> Q64 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子9岁了下颌骨后缩，以后能自己长好吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">9岁能看出下颌后缩的话，大概率是遗传因素比较大，还是去及早干预一下比较好。比如看是不是能够通过下颌引导或者其他的干预措施去刺激一下颌骨的发育。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q65 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子有多颗楔形齿还有龅牙，还能整牙吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">楔形齿用我们专业的叫法叫楔状缺损，它的主要发病机理不是刷牙习惯，而是咬合关系不正常。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">楔状缺损一般发生在牙颈部，是咬合关系不正常，局部受力过大，导致发生了应力疲劳，牙齿表面的硬组织碎裂、剥脱，牙齿的牙龈的位置有或深或浅的凹槽。比较深的楔状缺损会导致牙齿敏感、不舒适，这时候应该补。想彻底消除楔状缺损，需要通过矫正建立正常的牙齿咬合关系。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br mpa-from-tpl="t"></span></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">7</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #7AAD77;line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;font-size: 18px;">其他常见儿童口腔症状</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p><br mpa-from-tpl="t"></p><section style="font-size: 16px;"><section style="margin: 10px 8px;line-height: 2em;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(255, 254, 254, 0);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(239, 239, 239);"><section powered-by="xiumi.us"><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q66 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：小孩儿的牙龈经常红肿，喊疼，要怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙龈经常红肿，并且还疼，我猜应该是牙缝的问题。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">牙缝的问题有两种情况，最乐观的就是塞了牙之后引起的牙龈乳头炎，牙龈乳头炎才会让孩子疼到有这种烦扰，因为大部分小孩其实对这种小的困扰不会那么敏感。比这种情况更严重的，可能是引起了牙髓或者其他病变。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"> Q67 </span></strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子两个牙齿之间的牙龈突然肿大了，是什么原因？一刷牙就流血，这还怎么刷牙？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">两个牙齿间的牙龈突然肿大，大概率是那里有牙结石或者是有食物嵌塞，一定是有异物刺激的原因。可以去医院找找原因。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q68 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子总是口腔溃疡，舌头也溃疡怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这个是口腔的粘膜病，反复的口腔溃疡叫慢性阿弗他溃疡，这和每个人自身的身体机理和还有所处的状态有关，用中医的话来讲就是肝火比较旺。口腔溃疡比较严重的，可以用一些所谓的滋阴清热的茶叶。这种情况没有什么药能够一劳永逸。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q69 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子的上嘴皮里面总长小米粒儿一样的小泡，刚开始可能是咬的，但是生长得太频繁了，怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这叫粘液囊肿。黏液囊肿和孩子咬破嘴皮的行为紧密相关。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们80%～90%的唾液都是由腮腺分泌的，除此之外还有两个颌下腺和舌下腺之间的小唾液腺，其余的唾</span><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;">液是由遍布口腔黏膜的各种小的唾液腺分泌的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="color: rgb(63, 63, 63);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们有时候会不小心或者故意地去咬粘膜，就咬破了小唾液腺，进而形成了疤痕，疤痕把唾液腺分泌的导管口堵塞，唾液出不来就形成透明的小泡泡。有的孩子会再把它咬破，受损面再扩大。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">临床当中是要把它剥除的。牙医会剥出薄如蝉翼的小粘液囊肿，这时候是牙医们嘚瑟自己手艺的一个美好时刻。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">所以</span><strong><span style>不要让孩子去咬嘴唇、咬黏膜</span></strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 16px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;"> Q70 </span></strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：4岁的小朋友牙釉质发育不良，局部有脱矿，除了刷牙、涂氟，还有没有其他的保护建议？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">把牙刷得再认真一点。局部的脱矿就是牙菌斑，要特别认真的刷，之后一定要用牙菌斑指示剂。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q71 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：我家孩子6岁戴了一个预成冠，有没有副作用？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">戴预成冠应该是牙杀完神经后牙齿缺得比较严重的情况，育成冠是为了恢复孩子的咀嚼功能，保持间隙戴上的。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">杀了神经的牙一般不会正常脱落，会有两种情况：一种是该掉的时候不掉；一种是不该掉的时候提前掉了。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子6岁半，应该是乳磨牙。这种情况戴了育成冠我们也没办法观察他牙齿的动态，所以</span><span style="background-color: rgb(255, 254, 213);font-size: 16px;font-size: 16px;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">需要定期拍片子看孩子恒牙的萌出情况</span></strong></span><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">。牙齿如果脱落得不及时，有可能需要把它拔掉；如果过早松了，可能将来还要做一些间隙保持。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q72 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：有智齿什么时候拔最好?</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">最好的拔智齿年龄就是孩子正好高考以后，孩子17、18岁的样子。这个时候智齿正好发育2/3左右，是最好拔的状态；孩子恢复起来也是几乎没有任何后遗症的一种状态。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);color: rgb(255, 255, 255);"><strong> Q73 </strong></span><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：牙齿敏感怎么办？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">我们需要找病因：是牙齿的磨耗，还是牙颈部先天的牙齿剥脱或者缺失。</span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;line-height: 2em;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">轻微的可以涂一些脱敏剂；比较严重的看看有没有一些龋齿的原因，有时甚至是一些临面龋，是在牙龈下面牙缝的位置，我们看不到。那种有可能会冷热敏感，就需要治疗了。</span></p></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><section data-mpa-template="t" mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;width: 100%;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="background: rgb(252, 255, 247);border-radius: 26px 8px 8px 26px;border-width: 1px;border-style: dotted;border-color: rgb(16, 86, 58);display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><section style="width: 32px;height: 32px;background: #7AAD77;border-radius: 50% 50%;text-align: center;margin-left: 9px;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-size: 16px;font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, PingFang SC;font-weight: bold;color: #FFFFFF;line-height: 32px;" data-mid mpa-none-contnet="t">8</p></section><section style="padding: 0px 10px 0px 8px;height: 50px;text-align: center;" data-mid mpa-from-tpl="t"><p style="font-family: PingFangSC-Medium, "PingFang SC";font-weight: bold;color: rgb(122, 173, 119);line-height: 50px;" data-mid mpa-is-content="t"><span style="letter-spacing: 1px;">磨牙、门牙外凸、张嘴睡觉等</span></p></section></section></section></section></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q74 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子四岁，晚上使劲磨牙，这个需要干预吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">夜磨牙无论对于孩子还是成人都是一个疑难杂症。因为它没有清晰、具体的、单一的原因，多半是跟孩子的精神焦虑有关系。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q75 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子九岁了，总咬下嘴唇，门牙有点外凸，他的门牙外凸是因为总咬下嘴唇吗？需要去做矫正吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">咬嘴唇也会影响孩子的牙齿发育。咬嘴唇、咬铅笔、嘬手指头，这都是一些需要戒除的口腔不良习惯。已经很明显的话，需要去进行干预。最重要还是要把这个不良习惯戒除。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q76 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子张嘴睡觉的话，可以用胶带粘一下吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子张口呼吸需要去查一下具体的病因，孩子是有鼻炎还是有腺样体肥大？我们需要戒除的是孩子张口呼吸的病因。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">张口呼吸的确会导致我们的面部发育的异常，有一种异常叫腺样体面容，是这个样子的：</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><section style="text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;"><img class="rich_pages wxw-img js_insertlocalimg" data-backh="278" data-backw="578" data-ratio="0.48096192384769537" data-s="300,640" data-src="https://1-im.guokr.com/W0m7wuXwqRxR4rYF50EUuk75GOsN17d53qkPzshZPIPmAwAA4AEAAFBO.png" data-type="png" data-w="998" style="width: 100%;height: auto;" src="https://1-im.guokr.com/W0m7wuXwqRxR4rYF50EUuk75GOsN17d53qkPzshZPIPmAwAA4AEAAFBO.png?imageView2/1/w/555/h/266" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></section><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">这是典型的这个张口呼吸引起的腺样体面容，上牙弓又尖又窄，下颌后缩，这都是张口呼吸导致的口周肌群的失调。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">孩子的牙弓、牙齿发育异常，根本原因除了牙量和骨量的失调之外，最终牙齿的位置其实是我们舌肌和口周肌肉力量平衡的结果。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">张口呼吸的时候嘴是张着的，舌肌和口周肌肉的力量失衡，导致孩子的下颌不发育，上颌又窄又突，戒除病因才能避免将来孩子出现腺样体面容。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q77 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：孩子1岁半爱咬安抚巾对牙有没有影响？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><br></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">1岁半还好，基本上孩子3岁之前爱叼奶嘴、啃手指头，影响都不是特别大。只要不是一天到晚叼着不放都还好。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);background-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"> Q78 </span></strong><strong><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: 1px;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">：3岁的孩子喝奶还用奶瓶，这个会有影响吗？</span></strong></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">用奶瓶的问题不大，但是用完奶瓶之后要注意口腔清洁。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"><br></span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;">因为我们知道奶里面的含糖量都不低。喝奶之后尤其是喝夜奶，不做好清洁，很容易产生奶瓶龋。我见过的案例中，3、4岁孩子的20颗乳牙，坏18颗、坏20颗的都有。很严重的甚至需要全拔进行治疗。</span></p><p style="margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;line-height: 2em;text-align: justify;"><span style="font-family: "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(63, 63, 63);letter-spacing: 1px;"> </span></p><section
